is distributed across multiple JavaScript and C++ files. The entry point detection happens in lib/internal/modules/run_main.js through the shouldUseESMLoader() function, which determines if the main module should be loaded as ESM based on file extension, --experimental-default-type flag, and package.json type field. The core ModuleLoader class in lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js manages the module loading pipeline, maintaining a #resolveCache and loadCache for previously resolved and loaded modules. The loader uses ModuleJob and ModuleJobBase classes from lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js to track the loading state of individual modules and their dependencies over time. The _link() method in ModuleJob implements the linking/instantiation pipeline by retrieving module requests from ModuleWrap and recursively loading dependency modules. The resolve.js file implements the ESM specifier resolver with functions like defaultResolve() and specifier validation helpers (isBareSpecifier, isRelativeSpecifier), working alongside resolve.js's finalizeEsmResolution() function in the CJS loader for ESM fallback resolution. Module caching is managed by ResolveCache and LoadCache classes in lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js, which cache resolution results and loaded modules respectively. The translators system in lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js handles multiple module formats (json, wasm, commonjs, module), with format detection in get_format.js and formats.js providing mimeToFormat() and extensionFormatMap. The hooks system in hooks.js manages custom loader support. The load.js and fetch_module.js handle module source loading from file:// and data: URLs. The dynamic module creation is handled in create_dynamic_module.js, while import.meta initialization is done in initialize_import_meta.js. The native C++ ModuleWrap binding in src/module_wrap.cc and src/module_wrap.h provides the bridge to V8's module system, exposing methods for linking, instantiation, and evaluation of modules. The ModuleWrap class manages the V8 Module object and provides synchronous and asynchronous evaluation pathways. The utils.js file provides helper functions like getDefaultConditions() for ESM resolution conditions and compileSourceTextModule() for module compilation. Entry point ESM modules are detected and loaded through a coordination between run_main.js's shouldUseESMLoader(), the ModuleLoader instance, and ModuleJob, which ultimately delegates to ModuleWrap for actual V8 module instantiation and evaluation.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3350,"cache_read_input_tokens":76601,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3350},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ed62282c-36f4-4a0c-a8ea-cb493f23d69c","uuid":"9bb004d3-da7c-459a-86c4-8ba88fccabb1"}

is distributed across multiple JavaScript and C++ files. The entry point detection happens in lib/internal/modules/run_main.js through the shouldUseESMLoader() function, which determines if the main module should be loaded as ESM based on file extension, --experimental-default-type flag, and package.json type field. The core ModuleLoader class in lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js manages the module loading pipeline, maintaining a #resolveCache and loadCache for previously resolved and loaded modules. The loader uses ModuleJob and ModuleJobBase classes from lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js to track the loading state of individual modules and their dependencies over time. The _link() method in ModuleJob implements the linking/instantiation pipeline by retrieving module requests from ModuleWrap and recursively loading dependency modules. The resolve.js file implements the ESM specifier resolver with functions like defaultResolve() and specifier validation helpers (isBareSpecifier, isRelativeSpecifier), working alongside resolve.js's finalizeEsmResolution() function in the CJS loader for ESM fallback resolution. Module caching is managed by ResolveCache and LoadCache classes in lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js, which cache resolution results and loaded modules respectively. The translators system in lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js handles multiple module formats (json, wasm, commonjs, module), with format detection in get_format.js and formats.js providing mimeToFormat() and extensionFormatMap. The hooks system in hooks.js manages custom loader support. The load.js and fetch_module.js handle module source loading from file:// and data: URLs. The dynamic module creation is handled in create_dynamic_module.js, while import.meta initialization is done in initialize_import_meta.js. The native C++ ModuleWrap binding in src/module_wrap.cc and src/module_wrap.h provides the bridge to V8's module system, exposing methods for linking, instantiation, and evaluation of modules. The ModuleWrap class manages the V8 Module object and provides synchronous and asynchronous evaluation pathways. The utils.js file provides helper functions like getDefaultConditions() for ESM resolution conditions and compileSourceTextModule() for module compilation. Entry point ESM modules are detected and loaded through a coordination between run_main.js's shouldUseESMLoader(), the ModuleLoader instance, and ModuleJob, which ultimately delegates to ModuleWrap for actual V8 module instantiation and evaluation.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
